\doxysubsubsection{Detailed Description}
The model can compute various model related quantities based on symbolically generated code. 

Definition at line 77 of file model.\+h.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classamici_1_1_model_a0259cf8f0b132a25345ddc30c91febe8}\label{classamici_1_1_model_a0259cf8f0b132a25345ddc30c91febe8}} 
\index{Model@{Model}!computeX\_pos@{computeX\_pos}}
\index{computeX\_pos@{computeX\_pos}!Model@{Model}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{computeX\_pos()}{computeX\_pos()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily N\+\_\+\+Vector compute\+X\+\_\+pos (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const\+\_\+\+N\+\_\+\+Vector}]{x }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Compute non-\/negative state vector according to state\+Is\+Non\+Negative. If any\+State\+Non\+Negative is set to {\ttfamily false}, i.\+e., all entries in state\+Is\+Non\+Negative are {\ttfamily false}, this function directly returns {\ttfamily x}, otherwise all entries of x are copied in to {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classamici_1_1_model_ab9c5ab240fce621c2ccd2de6292c9260}{amici\+::\+Model\+::x\+\_\+pos\+\_\+tmp\+\_\+}}} and negative values are replaced by {\ttfamily 0} where applicable.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em x} & State vector possibly containing negative values \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
State vector with negative values replaced by {\ttfamily 0} according to state\+Is\+Non\+Negative 
\end{DoxyReturn}
